======================================================================
NAVMESH NAME HELPER CONTRACT AUDIT
======================================================================

Goal:
  Validate whether a central guard on 0x00690830 or 0x00690800 can safely turn invalid small endpoint pointers into a null identity.
  Runtime crash had ECX/EAX=0x00000004 and faulted on [ECX+0x1c], so this script focuses on helper callers and endpoint producers.
